You will listen to audio files generated by this application and translate individual phrases into a target language either in your mind or aloud. Resulting audio is divided into small paragraphs, each followed by a period of silence which gives you opportunity to summarize the paragraph in target language in your own words either in your mind or aloud. At the beginning, use short paragraphs, not longer than 300 characters because it will help you to remember more text of the original paragraph and thus to formulate your summary more easily.  \r\n\r\nYou can carry the audio files in your mp3 player or smartphone and therefore you can do the exercises on the go, when you are walking, jogging or doing some other menial tasks.  \r\n\r\nWhat is the suitable text? The difficulty of the text should correspond approximately to your proficiency in the target language. Use descriptive roundabout in your translation if you can, or simply move on and concentrate on the next phrase. The primary principle is to activate your passive vocabulary into the ability of fluent speaking, which requires diligent exercise. Precise translation of phrases or learning new words has secondary importance. Searching for words in a dictionary must be avoided because it means loss of time and concentration. In the real-life situations, there is no time for looking into dictionary anyway, so get used to it. During the second round of translation, you will probably be able to translate more phrases.
